A side effect of resetting the naming hierarchy is that even if you move the markup for the *NamingPanel* elements to a different *ContentPlaceholder* control, the rendered client IDs remain the same.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-571">請注意，則您必須確定呈現的控制項識別碼都是唯一的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-571">Note It is up to you to make sure that the rendered control IDs are unique.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-572">如果他們不這樣做，可能會中斷任何需要對個別的 HTML 項目，例如用戶端的唯一識別碼的功能*document.getElementById*函式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-572">If they are not, it can break any functionality that requires unique IDs for individual HTML elements, such as the client *document.getElementById* function.</span></span>


#### <a name="creating-predictable-client-ids-in-data-bound-controls"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-573">建立資料繫結控制項中的可預測的用戶端識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-573">Creating Predictable Client IDs in Data-Bound Controls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-574">*ClientID*所產生舊的演算法所資料繫結清單控制項中的控制項可以是值，且不是真的可預測。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-574">The *ClientID* values that are generated for controls in a data-bound list control by the legacy algorithm can be long and are not really predictable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-575">*ClientIDMode*功能可協助您將更多控制透過這些方式 Id 的產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-575">The *ClientIDMode* functionality can help you have more control over how these IDs are generated.</span></span>

### <a name="persisting-row-selection-in-data-controls"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-590">在資料控制項中的保存資料列選取範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-590">Persisting Row Selection in Data Controls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-591">*GridView*並*ListView*控制項可以讓使用者選取一個資料列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-591">The *GridView* and *ListView* controls can let users select a row.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-592">在舊版 ASP.NET 中，選取具有已根據頁面上的資料列索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-592">In previous versions of ASP.NET, selection has been based on the row index on the page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-593">比方說，如果您選取第 1 頁上的第三個項目，然後移至第 2 頁時，就會選取該頁面上的第三個項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-593">For example, if you select the third item on page 1 and then move to page 2, the third item on that page is selected.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-594">一開始只能在.NET Framework 3.5 SP1 中的動態資料專案中支援保存的選取項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-594">Persisted selection was initially supported only in Dynamic Data projects in the .NET Framework 3.5 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-595">啟用這項功能時，目前選取的項目根據項目的資料索引鍵。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-595">When this feature is enabled, the current selected item is based on the data key for the item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-596">這表示如果您選取第 1 頁的第三個資料列，並移至第 2 頁，不會選取在第 2 頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-596">This means that if you select the third row on page 1 and move to page 2, nothing is selected on page 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-597">當您移回至第 1 頁時，第三個資料列仍然會選取狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-597">When you move back to page 1, the third row is still selected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-598">現在支援保存的選取*GridView*並*ListView*使用的所有專案中的控制項*EnablePersistedSelection*屬性中所示下列範例：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-598">Persisted selection is now supported for the *GridView* and *ListView* controls in all projects by using the *EnablePersistedSelection* property, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-chart-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-599">ASP.NET 的 Chart 控制項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-599">ASP.NET Chart Control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-600">ASP.NET*圖表*控制項擴充.NET Framework 中的資料視覺效果供應項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-600">The ASP.NET *Chart* control expands the data-visualization offerings in the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-601">使用*圖表*控制項，您可以建立有直覺式且引人注目的圖表進行複雜的統計或財務分析的 ASP.NET 網頁。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-601">Using the *Chart* control, you can create ASP.NET pages that have intuitive and visually compelling charts for complex statistical or financial analysis.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-602">ASP.NET*圖表*控制項以.NET Framework 3.5 SP1 版中導入成 附加元件和是.NET Framework 4 版本的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-602">The ASP.NET *Chart* control was introduced as an add-on to the .NET Framework version 3.5 SP1 release and is part of the .NET Framework 4 release.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-603">控制項包含下列功能：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-603">The control includes the following features:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-604">35 種不同的圖表類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-604">35 distinct chart types.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-605">不限的數目的圖表區域、 標題、 圖例和附註。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-605">An unlimited number of chart areas, titles, legends, and annotations.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-606">各種不同的所有圖表項目的外觀設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-606">A wide variety of appearance settings for all chart elements.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-607">大部分的圖表類型支援 3d。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-607">3-D support for most chart types.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-608">可以自動配合資料點周圍的智慧型資料標籤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-608">Smart data labels that can automatically fit around data points.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-609">帶狀線、 刻度斷層和對數縮放比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-609">Strip lines, scale breaks, and logarithmic scaling.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-610">超過 50 種財務和統計公式可供資料分析與轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-610">More than 50 financial and statistical formulas for data analysis and transformation.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-611">簡單繫結和操作的圖表資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-611">Simple binding and manipulation of chart data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-612">常見的資料格式，例如日期、 時間和貨幣的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-612">Support for common data formats such as dates, times, and currency.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-613">支援互動性和事件驅動的自訂，包括用戶端按一下事件使用 Ajax。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-613">Support for interactivity and event-driven customization, including client click events using Ajax.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-614">狀態管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-614">State management.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-615">二進位資料流。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-615">Binary streaming.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-616">下圖顯示範例的財務 ASP.NET 的 Chart 控制項所產生的圖表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-616">The following figures show examples of financial charts that are produced by the ASP.NET Chart control.</span></span>

#### <a name="using-3-d-charts"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-623">使用 3d 圖表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-623">Using 3-D Charts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-624">*圖表*控制項包含*ChartAreas*集合，其中可以包含*ChartArea*定義特性的圖表區域的物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-624">The *Chart* control contains a *ChartAreas* collection, which can contain *ChartArea* objects that define characteristics of chart areas.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-625">例如，若要使用 3d 圖表區域中，使用*的 [area3dstyle]* 屬性，如下列範例所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-625">For example, to use 3-D for a chart area, use the *Area3DStyle* property as in the following example:</span></span>

### <a name="filtering-data-with-the-queryextender-control"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-635">QueryExtender 控制項使用的篩選資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-635">Filtering Data with the QueryExtender Control</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-636">建立資料導向的網頁開發人員的常見工作是篩選資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-636">A very common task for developers who create data-driven Web pages is to filter data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-637">這過去來執行建置*其中*子句中的資料來源控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-637">This traditionally has been performed by building *Where* clauses in data source controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-638">這種方法可能很複雜，在某些情況下*其中*語法不會讓您充分利用基礎資料庫的完整功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-638">This approach can be complicated, and in some cases the *Where* syntax does not let you take advantage of the full functionality of the underlying database.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-639">若要讓篩選更容易，新*QueryExtender* ASP.NET 4 中已加入控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-639">To make filtering easier, a new *QueryExtender* control has been added in ASP.NET 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-640">這個控制項可以加入至*EntityDataSource*或是*LinqDataSource*控制項，以篩選這些控制項所傳回的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-640">This control can be added to *EntityDataSource* or *LinqDataSource* controls in order to filter the data returned by these controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-641">因為*QueryExtender*控制項要依賴 LINQ、 將資料傳送至頁面上，會導致非常有效率的作業之前在資料庫伺服器上套用篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-641">Because the *QueryExtender* control relies on LINQ, the filter is applied on the database server before the data is sent to the page, which results in very efficient operations.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-642">*QueryExtender*控制項支援各種不同的篩選選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-642">The *QueryExtender* control supports a variety of filter options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-643">下列各節說明這些選項，並提供範例，示範如何使用它們。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-643">The following sections describe these options and provide examples of how to use them.</span></span>

#### <a name="search"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-644">搜尋</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-644">Search</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-647">範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-647">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-648">範圍選項類似於 [搜尋] 選項，但指定一組值來定義範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-648">The range option is similar to the search option, but specifies a pair of values to define the range.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-649">在下列範例中， *QueryExtender*控制搜尋`UnitPrice`傳回的資料中的資料行*LinqDataSource*控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-649">In the following example, the *QueryExtender* control searches the `UnitPrice` column in the data returned from the *LinqDataSource* control.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-650">範圍是讀取自 TextBoxFrom 和 TextBoxTo 控制項在頁面上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-650">The range is read from the TextBoxFrom and TextBoxTo controls on the page.</span></span>

### <a name="html-encoded-code-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-663">Html 編碼的程式碼運算式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-663">Html Encoded Code Expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-664">有些的 ASP.NET 網站 （特別是使用 ASP.NET MVC) 依賴使用`<%` =  `expression %>` （通常稱為 「 程式碼區塊 」） 的語法，將一些文字寫入回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-664">Some ASP.NET sites (especially with ASP.NET MVC) rely heavily on using `<%`= `expression %>` syntax (often called "code nuggets") to write some text to the response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-665">當您使用程式碼運算式時，很容易忘了將 HTML 編碼的文字，如果文字是來自使用者輸入，它可以保留頁面開啟 （跨網站指令碼） 的 XSS 攻擊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-665">When you use code expressions, it is easy to forget to HTML-encode the text, If the text comes from user input, it can leave pages open to an XSS (Cross Site Scripting) attack.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-666">ASP.NET 4 引進下列新的程式碼運算式語法：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-666">ASP.NET 4 introduces the following new syntax for code expressions:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample66.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-667">此語法會使用 HTML 編碼預設，寫入回應時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-667">This syntax uses HTML encoding by default when writing to the response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-668">這個新的運算式有效地將資料轉譯為下列：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-668">This new expression effectively translates to the following:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample67.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-669">比方說， &lt;%:要求 ["u"] %&gt;執行 HTML 編碼的值*要求 ["u"]*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-669">For example, &lt;%: Request["UserInput"] %&gt; performs HTML encoding on the value of *Request["UserInput"]*.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-670">這項功能的目標是讓舊語法的所有執行個體取代新語法，因此，您不強制每個步驟，決定要使用哪一個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-670">The goal of this feature is to make it possible to replace all instances of the old syntax with the new syntax so that you are not forced to decide at every step which one to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-671">不過，一些情況下所輸出的文字是 html 或已編碼，在此情況下這可能會導致重複編碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-671">However, there are cases in which the text being output is meant to be HTML or is already encoded, in which case this could lead to double encoding.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-672">針對這些情況下，ASP.NET 4 引進了新的介面*IHtmlString*的具象實作，以及*HtmlString*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-672">For those cases, ASP.NET 4 introduces a new interface, *IHtmlString*, along with a concrete implementation, *HtmlString*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-673">這些類型的執行個體可讓您表示，傳回的值是已正確編碼 （或否則檢查） 顯示為 HTML，並，因此值不應該經過 HTML 編碼一次。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-673">Instances of these types let you indicate that the return value is already properly encoded (or otherwise examined) for displaying as HTML, and that therefore the value should not be HTML-encoded again.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-674">例如，下列不應該 （和不） 編碼的 HTML:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-674">For example, the following should not be (and is not) HTML encoded:</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample68.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-675">ASP.NET MVC 2 的 helper 方法已在已更新為使用這種新語法，使它們不雙重編碼，但只當您執行 ASP.NET 4。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-675">ASP.NET MVC 2 helper methods have been updated to work with this new syntax so that they are not double encoded, but only when you are running ASP.NET 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-676">這種新語法無法運作時執行的應用程式使用 ASP.NET 3.5 SP1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-676">This new syntax does not work when you run an application using ASP.NET 3.5 SP1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-677">請注意這不保證 XSS 攻擊的保護。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-677">Keep in mind that this does not guarantee protection from XSS attacks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-678">例如，使用不在引號中的屬性值的 HTML 可以包含仍然容易受到影響的使用者輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-678">For example, HTML that uses attribute values that are not in quotation marks can contain user input that is still susceptible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-679">請注意，ASP.NET 控制項和 ASP.NET MVC 協助程式的輸出一律包含屬性值引號括起來，這是建議的方法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-679">Note that the output of ASP.NET controls and ASP.NET MVC helpers always includes attribute values in quotation marks, which is the recommended approach.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-680">同樣地，此語法不會執行 JavaScript 的編碼，例如當您建立 JavaScript 字串，根據使用者輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-680">Likewise, this syntax does not perform JavaScript encoding, such as when you create a JavaScript string based on user input.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429266"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304640"></a>

### <a name="project-template-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-681">專案範本的變更</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-681">Project Template Changes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-682">在舊版 ASP.NET 中，當您使用 Visual Studio 來建立新的網站專案或 Web 應用程式專案，產生的專案包含只 Default.aspx 頁面上，預設值`Web.config`檔案，而`App_Data`資料夾，如下列所示圖：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-682">In earlier versions of ASP.NET, when you use Visual Studio to create a new Web Site project or Web Application project, the resulting projects contain only a Default.aspx page, a default `Web.config` file, and the `App_Data` folder, as shown in the following illustration:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1A"></a>![](overview/_static/image4.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-683">Visual Studio 也支援空白網站專案型別，不包含任何檔案根本，如下圖所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-683">Visual Studio also supports an Empty Web Site project type, which contains no files at all, as shown in the following figure:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1B"></a>![](overview/_static/image5.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-684">結果是針對初學者，有極少的指引如何建置生產 Web 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-684">The result is that for the beginner, there is very little guidance on how to build a production Web application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-685">因此，ASP.NET 4 將介紹三個新的範本、 一個用於空的 Web 應用程式專案，以及分別指派給 Web 應用程式和網站專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-685">Therefore, ASP.NET 4 introduces three new templates, one for an empty Web application project, and one each for a Web Application and Web Site project.</span></span>

#### <a name="empty-web-application-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-686">空的 Web 應用程式範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-686">Empty Web Application Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-687">顧名思義，空白 Web 應用程式範本是精簡的 Web 應用程式專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-687">As the name suggests, the Empty Web Application template is a stripped-down Web Application project.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-688">選取此專案範本從 Visual Studio [新增專案] 對話方塊中，在下圖所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-688">You select this project template from the Visual Studio New Project dialog box, as shown in the following figure:</span></span>

[![](overview/_static/image7.png)](overview/_static/image6.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-689">([按一下以檢視完整大小的影像](overview/_static/image8.png))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-689">([Click to view full-size image](overview/_static/image8.png))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-690">當您建立空白的 ASP.NET Web 應用程式時，Visual Studio 會建立下列資料夾配置：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-690">When you create an Empty ASP.NET Web Application, Visual Studio creates the following folder layout:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1D"></a>![](overview/_static/image9.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-691">這是從舊版 ASP.NET 中，有一個例外狀況類似的空白網站配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-691">This is similar to the Empty Web Site layout from earlier versions of ASP.NET, with one exception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-692">在 Visual Studio 2010 中，空的 Web 應用程式和空白網站專案都包含下列最小`Web.config`檔案，其中包含 Visual Studio 用來識別專案目標 framework 的資訊：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-692">In Visual Studio 2010, Empty Web Application and Empty Web Site projects contain the following minimal `Web.config` file that contains information used by Visual Studio to identify the framework that the project is targeting:</span></span>

<a id="0.2_graphic1E"></a>![](overview/_static/image10.png)

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-693">如果沒有這麼做*targetFramework*屬性，若要開啟較舊的應用程式時，保留相容性目標.NET Framework 2.0 的 Visual Studio 預設值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-693">Without this *targetFramework* property, Visual Studio defaults to targeting the .NET Framework 2.0 in order to preserve compatibility when opening older applications.</span></span>

### <a name="css-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-722">CSS 增強功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-722">CSS Improvements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-723">ASP.NET 4 中重點之一就是工作的協助呈現 HTML 相容的最新的 HTML 標準。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-723">One of the major areas of work in ASP.NET 4 has been to help render HTML that is compliant with the latest HTML standards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-724">這包括 ASP.NET Web 伺服器控制項的 CSS 樣式的使用方式的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-724">This includes changes to how ASP.NET Web server controls use CSS styles.</span></span>

#### <a name="compatibility-setting-for-rendering"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-725">轉譯的相容性設定</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-725">Compatibility Setting for Rendering</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-726">根據預設，Web 應用程式或 Web 站台為目標的.NET Framework 4 中，當*controlRenderingCompatibilityVersion*屬性*頁*元素設定為"4.0"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-726">By default, when a Web application or Web site targets the .NET Framework 4, the *controlRenderingCompatibilityVersion* attribute of the *pages* element is set to "4.0".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-727">此項目會定義在電腦層級`Web.config`檔案，並根據預設會套用到所有的 ASP.NET 4 應用程式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-727">This element is defined in the machine-level `Web.config` file and by default applies to all ASP.NET 4 applications:</span></span>

[!code-xml[Main](overview/samples/sample69.xml)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-728">值*controlRenderingCompatibility*是一個字串，可讓潛在的新版本定義在未來的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-728">The value for *controlRenderingCompatibility* is a string, which allows potential new version definitions in future releases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-729">在目前的版本中，此屬性支援下列值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-729">In the current release, the following values are supported for this property:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-730">"3.5".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-730">"3.5".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-731">這個設定表示舊版轉譯和標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-731">This setting indicates legacy rendering and markup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-732">控制項所呈現的標記是 100%相容，以及設定*xhtmlConformance*屬性會接受。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-732">Markup rendered by controls is 100% backward compatible, and the setting of the *xhtmlConformance* property is honored.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-733">"4.0".</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-733">"4.0".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-734">如果屬性具有這項設定，ASP.NET Web 伺服器控制項執行下列作業：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-734">If the property has this setting, ASP.NET Web server controls do the following:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-735">*XhtmlConformance*屬性一律會視為"Strict"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-735">The *xhtmlConformance* property is always treated as "Strict".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-736">如此一來，控制項呈現的 XHTML 1.0 Strict 的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-736">As a result, controls render XHTML 1.0 Strict markup.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-737">停用非輸入控制項不再轉譯不正確的樣式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-737">Disabling non-input controls no longer renders invalid styles.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-738">*div*隱藏的欄位前後的項目現在的樣式，因此它們不會干擾使用者建立 CSS 規則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-738">*div* elements around hidden fields are now styled so they do not interfere with user-created CSS rules.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-739">功能表控制項呈現語意正確且符合協助工具指導方針的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-739">Menu controls render markup that is semantically correct and compliant with accessibility guidelines.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-740">驗證控制項不會轉譯內嵌樣式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-740">Validation controls do not render inline styles.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-741">控制先前呈現的框線 ="0"(衍生自 ASP.NET 控制項*表格*控制項，以及 ASP.NET*映像*控制項) 不再呈現此屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-741">Controls that previously rendered border="0" (controls that derive from the ASP.NET *Table* control, and the ASP.NET *Image* control) no longer render this attribute.</span></span>

#### <a name="disabling-controls"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-742">停用控制項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-742">Disabling Controls</span></span>

### <a name="hiding-div-elements-around-hidden-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-755">隱藏 div 周圍隱藏欄位的項目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-755">Hiding div Elements Around Hidden Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-756">ASP.NET 2.0 和更新版本的呈現系統特定隱藏的欄位 (例如*隱藏*用來儲存檢視狀態資訊的項目) 內*div*為了符合 XHTML 標準的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-756">ASP.NET 2.0 and later versions render system-specific hidden fields (such as the *hidden* element used to store view state information) inside *div* element in order to comply with the XHTML standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-757">不過，這可能會造成問題時的 CSS 規則會影響*div*頁面上的項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-757">However, this can cause a problem when a CSS rule affects *div* elements on a page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-758">例如，可能會導致頁面中出現一個像素列大約隱藏*div*項目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-758">For example, it can result in a one-pixel line appearing in the page around hidden *div* elements.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-759">在 ASP.NET 4 中， *div*括住 ASP.NET 產生的隱藏的欄位的項目新增 CSS 類別參考，如下列範例所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-759">In ASP.NET 4, *div* elements that enclose the hidden fields generated by ASP.NET add a CSS class reference as in the following example:</span></span>

[!code-html[Main](overview/samples/sample74.html)]

### <a name="rendering-an-outer-table-for-templated-controls"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-761">樣板化控制項呈現的外部資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-761">Rendering an Outer Table for Templated Controls</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-762">根據預設，下列的 ASP.NET Web 伺服器控制項支援範本自動包裝在外部資料表，可用來套用內嵌樣式：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-762">By default, the following ASP.NET Web server controls that support templates are automatically wrapped in an outer table that is used to apply inline styles:</span></span>

- *<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-763">FormView</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-763">FormView</span></span>*

### <a name="menu-control-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-800">功能表控制項的改善</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-800">Menu Control Improvements</span></span>

## <a name="aspnet-mvc"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-830">ASP.NET MVC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-830">ASP.NET MVC</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-831">ASP.NET MVC 是在 2009 年 3 月，做為附加元件架構引進到 ASP.NET 3.5 SP1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-831">ASP.NET MVC was introduced as an add-on framework to ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 in March 2009.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-832">Visual Studio 2010 包含 ASP.NET MVC 2，其中包含新特色與功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-832">Visual Studio 2010 includes ASP.NET MVC 2, which includes new features and capabilities.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429275"></a>

### <a name="areas-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-833">區域支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-833">Areas Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-834">區域可讓您群組控制器和檢視表到大型應用程式相對的獨立於其他區段的區段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-834">Areas let you group controllers and views into sections of a large application in relative isolation from other sections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-835">每個區域可以實作為個別的 ASP.NET MVC 專案，然後主應用程式參考。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-835">Each area can be implemented as a separate ASP.NET MVC project that can then be referenced by the main application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-836">這有助於管理複雜度，當您建置大型應用程式，並讓多個小組一起工作，在單一應用程式更容易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-836">This helps manage complexity when you build a large application and makes it easier for multiple teams to work together on a single application.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429276"></a>

### <a name="data-annotation-attribute-validation-support"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-837">資料註解屬性驗證支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-837">Data-Annotation Attribute Validation Support</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-838">*DataAnnotations*屬性可以讓您附加至模型的驗證邏輯使用中繼資料屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-838">*DataAnnotations* attributes let you attach validation logic to a model by using metadata attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-839">*DataAnnotations* ASP.NET 3.5 SP1 中的 ASP.NET Dynamic Data 中導入的屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-839">*DataAnnotations* attributes were introduced in ASP.NET Dynamic Data in ASP.NET 3.5 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-840">這些屬性已整合到預設模型繫結器，並提供中繼資料導向的方式，來驗證使用者輸入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-840">These attributes have been integrated into the default model binder and provide a metadata-driven means to validate user input.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429277"></a>

### <a name="templated-helpers"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-841">樣板化 Helper</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-841">Templated Helpers</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-842">樣板化 helper 可讓您自動產生關聯的編輯，並顯示與資料類型的範本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-842">Templated helpers let you automatically associate edit and display templates with data types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-843">比方說，您可以使用範本協助程式，來指定日期選擇器 UI 項目，如自動呈現*System.DateTime*值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-843">For example, you can use a template helper to specify that a date-picker UI element is automatically rendered for a *System.DateTime* value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-844">這是類似於 ASP.NET Dynamic Data 中的欄位範本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-844">This is similar to field templates in ASP.NET Dynamic Data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-845">*Html.EditorFor*並*Html.DisplayFor* helper 方法轉譯標準的資料類型以及複雜的物件，具有多個屬性，具有內建支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-845">The *Html.EditorFor* and *Html.DisplayFor* helper methods have built-in support for rendering standard data types as well as complex objects with multiple properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-846">它們也可讓您套用資料註解屬性，例如自訂轉譯*DisplayName*並*ScaffoldColumn*來*ViewModel*物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-846">They also customize rendering by letting you apply data-annotation attributes like *DisplayName* and *ScaffoldColumn* to the *ViewModel* object.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-847">通常您會想要自訂 UI 協助程式更進一步的輸出，並擁有完整控制權產生的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-847">Often you want to customize the output from UI helpers even further and have complete control over what is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-848">*Html.EditorFor*並*Html.DisplayFor* helper 方法支援此使用樣板化機制，可讓您定義可以覆寫的外部範本和控制項轉譯的輸出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-848">The *Html.EditorFor* and *Html.DisplayFor* helper methods support this using a templating mechanism that lets you define external templates that can override and control the output rendered.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-849">範本可以個別轉譯的類別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-849">The templates can be rendered individually for a class.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429278"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304649"></a>

## <a name="dynamic-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-850">Dynamic Data</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-850">Dynamic Data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-851">動態資料引進在 2008 年發行的.NET Framework 3.5 SP1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-851">Dynamic Data was introduced in the .NET Framework 3.5 SP1 release in mid-2008.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-852">這項功能提供了許多增強功能，來建立資料驅動應用程式，包括下列：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-852">This feature provides many enhancements for creating data-driven applications, including the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-853">快速建置資料導向網站 RAD 體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-853">A RAD experience for quickly building a data-driven Web site.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-854">資料模型中定義的條件約束為基礎的自動驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-854">Automatic validation that is based on constraints defined in the data model.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-855">能夠輕鬆地變更針對欄位中所產生的標記*GridView*並*DetailsView*使用動態資料專案一部分的欄位範本的控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-855">The ability to easily change the markup that is generated for fields in the *GridView* and *DetailsView* controls by using field templates that are part of your Dynamic Data project.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-856">請注意，如需詳細資訊，請參閱 <<c0> [ 動態資料文件](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx)MSDN Library 中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-856">Note For more information, see the [Dynamic Data documentation](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) in the MSDN Library.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-857">針對 ASP.NET 4 中，動態資料已經過增強，讓開發人員快速建置資料導向網站的更強大。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-857">For ASP.NET 4, Dynamic Data has been enhanced to give developers even more power for quickly building data-driven Web sites.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc253429279"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304650"></a>

### <a name="enabling-dynamic-data-for-existing-projects"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-858">對於現有的專案中啟用動態資料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-858">Enabling Dynamic Data for Existing Projects</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-859">隨附於.NET Framework 3.5 SP1 的動態資料功能帶入新的功能，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-859">Dynamic Data features that shipped in the .NET Framework 3.5 SP1 brought new features such as the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-860">欄位樣板 – 這些會提供資料類型為基礎的範本資料繫結控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-860">Field templates – These provide data-type-based templates for data-bound controls.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-861">欄位範本會提供更簡單的方式，來自訂比使用範本欄位的每個欄位的資料控制項的外觀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-861">Field templates provide a simpler way to customize the look of data controls than using template fields for each field.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-862">驗證-動態資料可讓您在資料類別上使用屬性來指定必要的欄位、 範圍檢查、 型別檢查、 使用規則運算式比對的模式的常見案例的驗證和自訂驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-862">Validation – Dynamic Data lets you use attributes on data classes to specify validation for common scenarios like required fields, range checking, type checking, pattern matching using regular expressions, and custom validation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-863">資料控制項，強制執行驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-863">Validation is enforced by the data controls.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-864">不過，這些功能有下列需求：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-864">However, these features had the following requirements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-865">資料存取層，就必須根據 Entity Framework 或 LINQ to SQL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-865">The data-access layer had to be based on Entity Framework or LINQ to SQL.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-866">唯一的資料來源支援這些功能的控制項*EntityDataSource*或是*LinqDataSource*控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-866">The only data source controls supported for these features were the *EntityDataSource* or *LinqDataSource* controls.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-867">功能需要 Web 專案以支援此功能所需的所有檔案使用的動態資料或動態資料實體範本所建立的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-867">The features required a Web project that had been created using the Dynamic Data or Dynamic Data Entities templates in order to have all the files that were required to support the feature.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-868">在 ASP.NET 4 中的動態資料支援，主要目的是啟用任何 ASP.NET 應用程式的動態資料的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-868">A major goal of Dynamic Data support in ASP.NET 4 is to enable the new functionality of Dynamic Data for any ASP.NET application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-869">下列範例顯示可以利用動態資料功能的現有網頁中的控制項的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-869">The following example shows markup for controls that can take advantage of Dynamic Data functionality in an existing page.</span></span>

[!code-aspx[Main](overview/samples/sample91.aspx)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-873">這項功能也提供其他好處，例如能夠指定預設值插入模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-873">This functionality also provides other benefits, such as being able to specify default values for insert mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-874">沒有動態的資料，來實作的預設值 欄位中，您必須附加至事件，找不到控制項 (使用*FindControl*)，並設定其值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-874">Without Dynamic Data, to implement a default value for a field, you must attach to an event, locate the control (using *FindControl*), and set its value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-875">在 ASP.NET 4 中， *EnableDynamicData*呼叫支援第二個參數，可讓您傳遞，在物件上的任何欄位的預設值，在此範例中所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-875">In ASP.NET 4, the *EnableDynamicData* call supports a second parameter that lets you pass default values for any field on the object, as shown in this example:</span></span>

### <a name="entity-templates"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-880">實體範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-880">Entity Templates</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-881">實體範本提供自訂的資料版面配置，而不需要您建立自訂頁面的新方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-881">Entity templates offer a new way to customize the layout of data without requiring you to create a custom page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-882">頁面上，使用範本*FormView*控制項 (而非*DetailsView*控制項，在舊版的動態資料的頁面範本中所使用) 和*DynamicEntity*要呈現實體範本的控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-882">Page templates use the *FormView* control (instead of the *DetailsView* control, as used in page templates in earlier versions of Dynamic Data) and the *DynamicEntity* control to render Entity templates.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-883">這可讓您更充分掌控 Dynamic Data 所呈現的標記。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-883">This gives you more control over the markup that is rendered by Dynamic Data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-884">下列清單顯示新的專案目錄配置，其中包含實體範本：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-884">The following list shows the new project directory layout that contains entity templates:</span></span>

### <a name="new-field-templates-for-urls-and-email-addresses"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-897">新的欄位範本 Url 和電子郵件地址</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-897">New Field Templates for URLs and Email Addresses</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-898">ASP.NET 4 引進了兩個新的內建欄位範本，`EmailAddress.ascx`和`Url.ascx`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-898">ASP.NET 4 introduces two new built-in field templates, `EmailAddress.ascx` and `Url.ascx`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-899">這些範本用於標示欄位*EmailAddress*或是*Url*使用*DataType*屬性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-899">These templates are used for fields that are marked as *EmailAddress* or *Url* with the *DataType* attribute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-900">針對*EmailAddress*物件時，欄位會顯示為超連結建立利用*mailto:* 通訊協定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-900">For *EmailAddress* objects, the field is displayed as a hyperlink that is created by using the *mailto:* protocol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-901">當使用者按一下連結時，它會開啟使用者的電子郵件用戶端的連線，並建立基本架構的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-901">When users click the link, it opens the user's email client and creates a skeleton message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-902">物件的型別為*Url*會顯示為一般的超連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-902">Objects typed as *Url* are displayed as ordinary hyperlinks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-903">下列範例會顯示欄位會標示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-903">The following example shows how fields would be marked.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[Main](overview/samples/sample100.cs)]

### <a name="support-for-inheritance-in-the-data-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-910">支援的資料模型中的繼承</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-910">Support for Inheritance in the Data Model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-911">Entity Framework 和 LINQ to SQL 支援繼承其資料模型中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-911">Both the Entity Framework and LINQ to SQL support inheritance in their data models.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-912">這個範例可能是資料庫具有`InsurancePolicy`資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-912">An example of this might be a database that has an `InsurancePolicy` table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-913">它可能也包含`CarPolicy`並`HousePolicy`具有相同的欄位的資料表，`InsurancePolicy`然後新增更多的欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-913">It might also contain `CarPolicy` and `HousePolicy` tables that have the same fields as `InsurancePolicy` and then add more fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-914">動態資料已經過修改，以了解資料模型中的繼承的物件，以及繼承的資料表支援 scaffolding。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-914">Dynamic Data has been modified to understand inherited objects in the data model and to support scaffolding for the inherited tables.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729048"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429285"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304656"></a>

### <a name="support-for-many-to-many-relationships-entity-framework-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-915">支援多對多關聯性 (Entity Framework)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-915">Support for Many-to-Many Relationships (Entity Framework Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-916">Entity Framework 提供豐富的支援，藉由在上公開為集合關聯性的資料表之間的多對多關聯性*實體*物件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-916">The Entity Framework has rich support for many-to-many relationships between tables, which is implemented by exposing the relationship as a collection on an *Entity* object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-917">新`ManyToMany.ascx`和`ManyToMany_Edit.ascx`欄位範本已新增至可顯示和編輯多對多關聯性中涉及的資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-917">New `ManyToMany.ascx` and `ManyToMany_Edit.ascx` field templates have been added to provide support for displaying and editing data that is involved in many-to-many relationships.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729049"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429286"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304657"></a>

### <a name="new-attributes-to-control-display-and-support-enumerations"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-918">新的屬性，以控制顯示，並支援列舉</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-918">New Attributes to Control Display and Support Enumerations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-919">*DisplayAttribute*已新增，讓您進一步控制欄位的顯示方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-919">The *DisplayAttribute* has been added to give you additional control over how fields are displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-920">*DisplayName*屬性在舊版的動態資料允許您變更用來當做標題欄位的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-920">The *DisplayName* attribute in earlier versions of Dynamic Data allowed you to change the name that is used as a caption for a field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-921">新*DisplayAttribute*類別可讓您指定多個選項來顯示一個欄位，例如欄位會顯示以及是否將使用欄位作為篩選條件的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-921">The new *DisplayAttribute* class lets you specify more options for displaying a field, such as the order in which a field is displayed and whether a field will be used as a filter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-922">屬性也會提供獨立的使用中的標籤名稱的控制項*GridView*控制項，用於的名稱*DetailsView*控制項，[] 欄位中的說明文字和浮水印用於欄位 （如果欄位可接受文字輸入）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-922">The attribute also provides independent control of the name used for the labels in a *GridView* control, the name used in a *DetailsView* control, the help text for the field, and the watermark used for the field (if the field accepts text input).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-923">*EnumDataTypeAttribute*類別已新增可讓您將欄位對應至列舉型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-923">The *EnumDataTypeAttribute* class has been added to let you map fields to enumerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-924">當您將這個屬性套用至欄位時，您會指定列舉型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-924">When you apply this attribute to a field, you specify an enumeration type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-925">使用新的動態資料`Enumeration.ascx`建立 UI，來顯示和編輯列舉值的欄位樣板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-925">Dynamic Data uses the new `Enumeration.ascx` field template to create UI for displaying and editing enumeration values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-926">範本會對應資料庫中的值給列舉型別中的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-926">The template maps the values from the database to the names in the enumeration.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729050"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429287"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304658"></a>

### <a name="enhanced-support-for-filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-927">篩選器的增強的支援</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-927">Enhanced Support for Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-928">動態資料 1.0 隨附內建布林資料行和外部索引鍵資料行的篩選器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-928">Dynamic Data 1.0 shipped with built-in filters for Boolean columns and foreign-key columns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-929">篩選不允許您指定是否已顯示，請將它們，或它們所顯示的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-929">The filters did not allow you to specify whether they were displayed or in what order they were displayed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-930">新*DisplayAttribute*屬性的地址這兩個這些問題，讓您控制是否顯示資料行做為篩選條件和順序將會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-930">The new *DisplayAttribute* attribute addresses both of these issues by giving you control over whether a column is displayed as a filter and in what order it will be displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-931">其他的增強功能是篩選支援已經過重新[編寫成使用新](#0.2__QueryExtender "_QueryExtender") Web Form 的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-931">An additional enhancement is that filtering support has been re[written to use the new](#0.2__QueryExtender "_QueryExtender") feature of Web Forms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-932">這可讓您建立篩選器，而不需要篩選器可搭配資料來源控制項的知識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-932">This lets you create filters without requiring knowledge of the data source control that the filters will be used with.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-933">這些擴充功能，以及篩選有也已轉換成範本的控制項，可讓您新增新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-933">Along with these extensions, filters have also been turned into template controls, which allows you to add new ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-934">最後， *DisplayAttribute*先前所述的類別可讓預設篩選，以覆寫，在同一個採用的方式*UIHint*允許覆寫的資料行的預設欄位樣板。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-934">Finally, the *DisplayAttribute* class mentioned earlier allows the default filter to be overridden, in the same way that *UIHint* allows the default field template for a column to be overridden.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729051"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429288"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304659"></a>

## <a name="visual-studio-2010-web-development-improvements"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-935">Visual Studio 2010 Web 開發方面的改進</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-935">Visual Studio 2010 Web Development Improvements</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729052"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429289"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304660"></a>

### <a name="improved-css-compatibility"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-937">改良的 CSS 相容性</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-937">Improved CSS Compatibility</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-938">Visual Web Developer 設計工具，Visual Studio 2010 中的有已更新並改良 CSS 2.1 標準相容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-938">The Visual Web Developer designer in Visual Studio 2010 has been updated to improve CSS 2.1 standards compliance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-939">設計工具更好會保留的 HTML 原始檔的完整性，並且會比在舊版的 Visual Studio 更健全。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-939">The designer better preserves integrity of the HTML source and is more robust than in previous versions of Visual Studio.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-940">在幕後，架構也進行了改進的就是好讓未來的增強功能，在轉譯、 版面配置，與服務性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-940">Under the hood, architectural improvements have also been made that will better enable future enhancements in rendering, layout, and serviceability.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729053"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429290"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304661"></a>

### <a name="html-and-javascript-snippets"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-941">HTML 和 JavaScript 程式碼片段</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-941">HTML and JavaScript Snippets</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-942">在 HTML 編輯器中，IntelliSense 自動完成標記名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-942">In the HTML editor, IntelliSense auto-completes tag names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-943">IntelliSense 程式碼片段功能會自動完成整個標籤和更多功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-943">The IntelliSense Snippets feature auto-completes entire tags and more.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-944">在 Visual Studio 2010 中，JavaScript 與 C# 和 Visual Basic 中，不支援在舊版的 Visual Studio 支援 IntelliSense 程式碼片段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-944">In Visual Studio 2010, IntelliSense snippets are supported for JavaScript, alongside C# and Visual Basic, which were supported in earlier versions of Visual Studio.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-945">Visual Studio 2010 包含 200 多個程式碼片段，協助您自動完成一般 ASP.NET 和 HTML 標記，包括必要的屬性 (例如 runat ="server") 和標記特有的通用屬性 (例如*識別碼*， *DataSourceID*， *ControlToValidate*，以及*文字*)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-945">Visual Studio 2010 includes over 200 snippets that help you auto-complete common ASP.NET and HTML tags, including required attributes (such as runat="server") and common attributes specific to a tag (such as *ID*, *DataSourceID*, *ControlToValidate*, and *Text*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-946">您可以下載其他程式碼片段，或您可以撰寫您自己片段，可封裝您或您的小組使用的常見工作的標記區塊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-946">You can download additional snippets, or you can write your own snippets that encapsulate the blocks of markup that you or your team use for common tasks.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729054"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429291"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304662"></a>

### <a name="javascript-intellisense-enhancements"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-947">JavaScript IntelliSense 的增強功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-947">JavaScript IntelliSense Enhancements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-948">在 Visual 2010 中，JavaScript IntelliSense 已重新設計，提供更豐富的編輯體驗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-948">In Visual 2010, JavaScript IntelliSense has been redesigned to provide an even richer editing experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-949">IntelliSense 現在會表彰動態產生的方法這類的物件*registerNamespace*和其他 JavaScript 架構所使用的類似技術。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-949">IntelliSense now recognizes objects that have been dynamically generated by methods such as *registerNamespace* and by similar techniques used by other JavaScript frameworks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-950">已改善效能，分析大型的程式庫的指令碼，並顯示幾乎沒有任何處理延遲的 IntelliSense。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-950">Performance has been improved to analyze large libraries of script and to display IntelliSense with little or no processing delay.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-951">為支援幾乎所有的協力廠商程式庫，並支援各種不同的編碼樣式已大幅增加相容性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-951">Compatibility has been dramatically increased to support nearly all third-party libraries and to support diverse coding styles.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-952">當您輸入，並立即利用 IntelliSense，現在會剖析文件註解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-952">Documentation comments are now parsed as you type and are immediately leveraged by IntelliSense.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729055"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429292"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304663"></a>

## <a name="web-application-deployment-with-visual-studio-2010"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-953">使用 Visual Studio 2010 的 web 應用程式部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-953">Web Application Deployment with Visual Studio 2010</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-954">當 ASP.NET 開發人員部署 Web 應用程式時，他們經常遇到問題，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-954">When ASP.NET developers deploy a Web application, they often find that they encounter issues such as the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-955">部署到共用裝載站台需要技術，例如 FTP，可能會很慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-955">Deploying to a shared hosting site requires technologies such as FTP, which can be slow.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-956">此外，您必須手動執行工作，例如執行 SQL 指令碼，以設定資料庫，而且您必須變更 IIS 設定，例如做為應用程式中設定虛擬目錄資料夾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-956">In addition, you must manually perform tasks such as running SQL scripts to configure a database and you must change IIS settings, such as configuring a virtual directory folder as an application.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-957">在企業環境中，除了部署 Web 應用程式檔案中，系統管理員通常必須修改 ASP.NET 組態檔和 IIS 設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-957">In an enterprise environment, in addition to deploying the Web application files, administrators frequently must modify ASP.NET configuration files and IIS settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-958">資料庫管理員必須執行一系列的 SQL 指令碼，以取得執行的應用程式資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-958">Database administrators must run a series of SQL scripts to get the application database running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-959">這類安裝大量的人力，通常需要較小時才能完成，且必須仔細記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-959">Such installations are labor intensive, often take hours to complete, and must be carefully documented.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-960">Visual Studio 2010 包含的技術，以解決這些問題，並讓您順暢地部署 Web 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-960">Visual Studio 2010 includes technologies that address these issues and that let you seamlessly deploy Web applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-961">這些技術的其中之一是 IIS Web Deployment Tool (MsDeploy.exe)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-961">One of these technologies is the IIS Web Deployment Tool (MsDeploy.exe).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-962">Visual Studio 2010 中的 web 部署功能包括下列重點：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-962">Web deployment features in Visual Studio 2010 include the following major areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-963">Web 封裝</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-963">Web packaging</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-964">Web.config 轉換</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-964">Web.config transformation</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-965">資料庫部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-965">Database deployment</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-966">單鍵發行為 Web 應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-966">One-click publish for Web applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-967">下列各節提供有關這些功能的詳細資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-967">The following sections provide details about these features.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729056"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429293"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304664"></a>

### <a name="web-packaging"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-968">Web 封裝</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-968">Web Packaging</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-969">Visual Studio 2010 使用 MSDeploy 工具，來建立您的應用程式，這指的壓縮 (.zip) 檔案*網頁套件*。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-969">Visual Studio 2010 uses the MSDeploy tool to create a compressed (.zip) file for your application, which is referred to as a *Web package*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-970">封裝檔案會包含您的應用程式加上下列內容的相關中繼資料：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-970">The package file contains metadata about your application plus the following content:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-971">IIS 設定，其中包括應用程式集區設定、 錯誤頁面設定，等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-971">IIS settings, which includes application pool settings, error page settings, and so on.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-972">實際的 Web 內容，其中包含 Web 網頁、 使用者控制項、 靜態內容 （映像和 HTML 檔案），等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-972">The actual Web content, which includes Web pages, user controls, static content (images and HTML files), and so on.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-973">SQL Server 資料庫結構描述和資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-973">SQL Server database schemas and data.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-974">安全性憑證，將安裝在 GAC、 登錄設定等等的元件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-974">Security certificates, components to install in the GAC, registry settings, and so on.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-975">網頁套件可以複製到任何伺服器，並再使用 IIS 管理員以手動方式安裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-975">A Web package can be copied to any server and then installed manually by using IIS Manager.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-976">或者，用於自動化部署，封裝可以安裝使用命令列命令，或使用部署 Api。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-976">Alternatively, for automated deployment, the package can be installed by using command-line commands or by using deployment APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-977">Visual Studio 2010 提供內建的 MSBuild 工作與建立 Web 封裝的目標。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-977">Visual Studio 2010 provides built in MSBuild tasks and targets to create Web packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-978">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 < [ASP.NET Web 應用程式專案部署概觀](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd394698%28VS.100%29.aspx)MSDN 網站上並[10 + 20 的原因，為什麼您應該建立網頁套件](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/07/10-20-reasons-why-you-should-create-web.html)Vishal Joshi 部落格上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-978">For more information, see [ASP.NET Web Application Project Deployment Overview](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd394698%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [10 + 20 reasons why you should create a Web Package](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/07/10-20-reasons-why-you-should-create-web.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729057"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429294"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304665"></a>

### <a name="webconfig-transformation"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-979">Web.config 轉換</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-979">Web.config Transformation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-980">部署 Web 應用程式，Visual Studio 2010 推出[XML 文件轉換 (XDT)](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)，這是一個功能，可讓您轉換`Web.config`開發設定生產環境設定的檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-980">For Web application deployment, Visual Studio 2010 introduces [XML Document Transform (XDT)](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html), which is a feature that lets you transform a `Web.config` file from development settings to production settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-981">轉換設定會指定於名為轉換檔案`web.debug.config`， `web.release.config`，依此類推。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-981">Transformation settings are specified in transform files named `web.debug.config`, `web.release.config`, and so on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-982">（這些檔案的名稱符合 MSBuild 組態）。轉換檔包含只變更，您必須先部署`Web.config`檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-982">(The names of these files match MSBuild configurations.) A transform file includes just the changes that you need to make to a deployed `Web.config` file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-983">您可以使用簡單的語法，以指定所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-983">You specify the changes by using simple syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-984">下列範例會顯示部分`web.release.config`部署您的發行設定檔可能會產生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-984">The following example shows a portion of a `web.release.config` file that might be produced for deployment of your release configuration.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-985">取代關鍵字，在範例中所指定的是，在部署期間*connectionString*中的節點`Web.config`檔案將會取代此範例中所列的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-985">The Replace keyword in the example specifies that during deployment the *connectionString* node in the `Web.config` file will be replaced with the values that are listed in the example.</span></span>

[!code-xml[Main](overview/samples/sample102.xml)]

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-986">如需詳細資訊，請參閱 < [Web 應用程式專案部署的 Web.config 轉換語法](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465326%28VS.100%29.aspx)msdn <a id="0.2_a"> </a>的網站和[Web 部署：Web.Config 轉換](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)Vishal Joshi 部落格上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-986">For more information, see [Web.config Transformation Syntax for Web Application Project Deployment](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465326%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN <a id="0.2_a"></a> Web site and[Web Deployment: Web.Config Transformation](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729058"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429295"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304666"></a>

### <a name="database-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-987">資料庫部署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-987">Database Deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-988">Visual Studio 2010 的部署套件可以包含在 SQL Server 資料庫上的相依性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-988">A Visual Studio 2010 deployment package can include dependencies on SQL Server databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-989">封裝定義的一部分中,，您可以提供連接字串的來源資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-989">As part of the package definition, you provide the connection string for your source database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-990">當您建立的 Web 套件時，Visual Studio 2010 建立 SQL 指令碼的資料庫結構描述以及選擇性的資料，並再將這些封裝。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-990">When you create the Web package, Visual Studio 2010 creates SQL scripts for the database schema and optionally for the data, and then adds these to the package.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-991">您也可以提供自訂的 SQL 指令碼，並指定在伺服器應該執行的順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-991">You can also provide custom SQL scripts and specify the sequence in which they should run on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-992">您可以在部署期間提供適用於目標伺服器的連接字串部署程序接著會使用此連接字串執行的指令碼所建立的資料庫結構描述並加入資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-992">At deployment time, you provide a connection string that is appropriate for the target server; the deployment process then uses this connection string to run the scripts that create the database schema and add the data.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-993">此外，使用單鍵發行，您可以設定部署至應用程式發佈到遠端共用裝載站台時，直接發佈您的資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-993">In addition, by using one-click publish, you can configure deployment to publish your database directly when the application is published to a remote shared hosting site.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-994">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[如何：部署資料庫與 Web 應用程式專案](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465343%28VS.100%29.aspx)MSDN 網站上並[VS 2010 中的資料庫部署](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html)Vishal Joshi 部落格上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-994">For more information, see [How to: Deploy a Database With a Web Application Project](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465343%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [Database Deployment with VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/03/web-deployment-webconfig-transformation_23.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

<a id="0.2__Toc224729059"></a><a id="0.2__Toc253429296"></a><a id="0.2__Toc243304667"></a>

### <a name="one-click-publish-for-web-applications"></a><span data-ttu-id="7ab76-995">單鍵發行為 Web 應用程式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-995">One-Click Publish for Web Applications</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-996">Visual Studio 2010 也可讓您使用 IIS 遠端管理服務發佈至遠端伺服器的 Web 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-996">Visual Studio 2010 also lets you use the IIS remote management service to publish a Web application to a remote server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-997">針對您的裝載帳戶或測試伺服器或臨時伺服器，您可以建立發行設定檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-997">You can create a publish profile for your hosting account or for testing servers or staging servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-998">每個設定檔可以安全地儲存適當的認證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-998">Each profile can save appropriate credentials securely.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-999">然後您可以部署到任何目標伺服器，只要按一下，使用 Web 單鍵發行工具列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-999">You can then deploy to any of the target servers with one click by using the Web one-click publish toolbar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1000">Visual Studio 2010 中，您也可以使用 MSBuild 命令列發佈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1000">With Visual Studio 2010, you can also publish by using the MSBuild command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1001">這可讓您設定持續整合模型中包含發行您小組的建置環境。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1001">This lets you configure your team build environment to include publishing in a continuous-integration model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1002">如需詳細資訊，請參閱[如何：部署 Web 應用程式專案使用單鍵發行和 Web Deploy](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465337%28VS.100%29.aspx) MSDN 網站上並[Web 1-按一下發佈與 VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/05/web-1-click-publish-with-vs-2010.html) Vishal Joshi 部落格上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1002">For more information, see [How to: Deploy a Web Application Project Using One-Click Publish and Web Deploy](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/dd465337%28VS.100%29.aspx) on the MSDN Web site and [Web 1-Click Publish with VS 2010](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2009/05/web-1-click-publish-with-vs-2010.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1003">若要檢視 Visual Studio 2010 中的 Web 應用程式部署相關的視訊簡報，請參閱[VS 2010 進行 Web 開發人員預覽](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2008/12/vs-2010-for-web-developer-previews.html)Vishal Joshi 部落格上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1003">To view video presentations about Web application deployment in Visual Studio 2010, see [VS 2010 for Web Developer Previews](http://vishaljoshi.blogspot.com/2008/12/vs-2010-for-web-developer-previews.html) on Vishal Joshi's blog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1007">[https://www.asp.net/](https://www.asp.net/) -ASP.NET 小組自己的網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1007">[https://www.asp.net/](https://www.asp.net/) — The ASP.NET team's own Web site.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="7ab76-1008">[https://www.asp.net/dynamicdata/](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) 並[ASP.NET 動態資料內容對應](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545%28VS.100%29.aspx)— ASP.NET 小組網站和 ASP.NET Dynamic Data 的官方文件中的線上資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="7ab76-1008">[https://www.asp.net/dynamicdata/](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545.aspx) and [ASP.NET Dynamic Data Content Map](https://msdn.microsoft.com/library/cc488545%28VS.100%29.aspx) — Online resources on the ASP.NET team site and in the official documentation for ASP.NET Dynamic Data.</span></span>
